[30;1m89 | [0m[35m-------------------------[0m
[30;1m90 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m91 | [0m[35mHDMF uses setuptools_scm_ for versioning source and wheel distributions. `setuptools_scm` creates a [0m
[30;1m92 | [0m[35mname for the wheels that are created based on git tags.[0m
[30;1m93 | [0m[35mAfter all the tests pass, the "Deploy release" GitHub Actions workflow[0m
